# Welcome To The Air University
Air University empowers students to explore their potential, excel academically, and shape the future with confidence. 
[Admission Now](https://webdata.au.edu.pk/Pages/Admission/admission_advertisement.aspx) [View Program](https://www.au.edu.pk/#program-sec)
# Why Air University ?
Air University empowers you with quality education, real-world skills, and a supportive community dedicated to helping you excel and lead with confidence
[Admission Now](https://www.au.edu.pk/) [View Program](https://www.au.edu.pk/)
# Air University National And Global Ranking
It is 2nd place in National Ranking and 1009 in Best Global Universities by U.S. News & World Report 
# Mission and Vision of Air University
Air University aims to foster excellence in education and research, developing graduates with knowledge, integrity, and social responsibility for a better society.

About Us
## Welcome to Air University
We are committed to leave the world a better place. We pursue new technology, encourage creativity, engage with our communities, and share an entrepreneurial mindset.
### Why Air University ?
Air University empowers you with quality education and real-world skills.
### National and Global Ranking
It is ranked at 2nd Position at national level and 1009 in Best Global Universities by U.S. News & World Report

delivering quality education, fostering research and innovation, and shaping leaders who contribute positively to society.

### [Usama Bin Sabir](https://www.au.edu.pk/)
"PhD Scholar in Agricultural Robotics at Cornell University, USA, recognized as the first Airian to reach Cornell, representing Air University on a global academic platform."
### [Usama Bin Sabir](https://www.au.edu.pk/)
### [Mehvish Anwar](https://www.au.edu.pk/)
"Aircraft Maintenance Engineer at Pakistan International Airlines (PIA), holding the distinction of being PIA‚Äôs first female flying spanner engineer, a historic milestone for women in aviation engineering in Pakistan."
### [Mehvish Anwar](https://www.au.edu.pk/)
### [Hassaan Iqbal](https://www.au.edu.pk/)
"Assistant Director, Student Support at Air University. Actively involved in student support and institutional operations, with a strong commitment to philanthropy and social impact. Former President of the AU Blood Donor Society and Security Team, Vice President of the AU Islamic Society, and Founder of the Corporate Social Responsibility Society."
### [Hassaan Iqbal](https://www.au.edu.pk/)
### [Syeda Wazish Zahra](https://www.au.edu.pk/)
"Former Programme Specialist with UNICEF and other humanitarian organizations. Brings 14+ years of experience in monitoring, data analysis, and community-based development programs."
### [Syeda Wazish Zahra](https://www.au.edu.pk/)
### [Maryam Nisar](https://www.au.edu.pk/)
"Commercial Director at Jazz, leading the organization‚Äôs largest revenue-generating region with annual business exceeding USD 200M. Brings 15 years of experience across sales, marketing, fintech, AI, FMCG, P&L management, and digital transformation. Actively mentors startups through Hatch Pakistan and holds executive certifications from INSEAD and LUMS."
### [Maryam Nisar](https://www.au.edu.pk/)
### [Salman Ahmad Bhutta](https://www.au.edu.pk/)
"MS Scholar in Nuclear and Subnuclear Physics at Alma Mater Studiorum ‚Äì University of Bologna, Italy, representing Pakistan internationally. Founder of Air Astronomical Society and Bayt al-Hikmah; led initiatives including NASA Space Apps Challenge (Islamabad), World Space Week, and CERN outreach; author of Some Unstitched Words. Recipient of Most Promising AIRian of the Year 2025, Vice Chancellor‚Äôs Letter of Recognition, national awards, and multiple merit-based scholarships. Actively mentoring students globally as International Student Ambassador and Italy Chapter Lead of AU Alumni."
### [Salman Ahmad Bhutta](https://www.au.edu.pk/)

# URL: https://portals.au.edu.pk/aujogr

#### Air University Journal of Graduate Research


  

# A Platform For Graduate Students' Research
#### Welcome to the webpage of AU JoGR an online journal providing a platform for graduate students to present their research to write high quality papers and to form linkages with researchers of similar interests.
#### Papers are invited in all disciplines offered at Air University including Sciences and Engineering, the Social Sciences (Humanities, Education and Psychology), Strategic Studies, Management and Finance.
#### To submit your work, please see the [Word Template ](https://au.edu.pk/Pages/Graduate_Studies/documents/Standardized_Thesis_Template/AUJoGRTemplate.docx)for submission of your Manuscript.

## About the Journal
JOURNAL OF BUSINESS & ECONOMICS (JBE)
ISSN (print): 2075-6909 | ISSN (online): 2708-1923. Frequency: Bi-annual (June and December)
Chief Editor: Professor Dr. Habib Ahmed,
Managing Editor: Dr. Muzammel Shah. 
Associate Editor: Ms. Sana Farzand Ali
Journal of Business & Economics (JBE) is an internationally refereed, peer-reviewed academic journal with an aim of publishing research that has a strong theoretical and empirical contribution. The first issue of JBE was published in 2009 by the Faculty of Administrative Sciences, Air University, Islamabad. Since then, it is regularly published in volumes with two issues, i.e., January-June and July-December. The journal provides an opportunity to develop a strong basis for conceptual and professional growth by sharing the latest research findings and best practices.
##  Current Issue 
Vol. 17 No. 1 (2025): Journal of Business & Economics (JBE) 
Journal of Business & Economics (JBE) is an internationally refereed, peer-reviewed academic journal to publishes research that has strong theoretical and empirical contributions. The first issue of JBE was published in 2009 by the Faculty of Administrative Sciences, Air University, Islamabad. Since then it has been regularly published in volumes with two issues i.e. January-June and July-December. The journal provides an opportunity to develop a strong basis for conceptual and professional growth by sharing the latest research findings and best practices.
Published:  2025-06-30

###  The Department of Computer Science at Air University Aerospace & Aviation Campus Kamra students went on industrial visit to Systems Limited (Amazon Office) located in DHA Phase 2 Islamabad. 
###  The Department of Computer Science, Air University Kamra, successfully hosted the AU Industry‚ÄìAcademia Innovation Summit 2025 & FYP-II Poster Exhibition.

### Students from the Electrical and Avionics Engineering Department, Air University Aerospace & Aviation Campus Kamra, visited the Independent System Market Operator (ISMO) Pakistan for an industrial study tour.
### Mr. Bakht Muhammad Khan, PhD Scholar in Electrical Engineering at Air University Aerospace & Aviation Campus, Kamra, under the supervision of Dr. Shahbaz Khan and Co-Supervision: Dr. Husan Ali, has successfully defended his doctoral dissertation titled ‚ÄúAdaptive Protection Scheme for Multi-Loop Power System Using Optimization Techniques.‚Äù

## Director's Campus Message
I look forward to you joining the ‚Äòcommunity‚Äô of Aerospace & Aviation Campus which is driven by energy of its vision of excellence in learning, research, innovation and public service. At AU-A&AC, you will feel empowered to realize your academic ambitions and seek out knowledge with purpose in fields ranging from basic sciences to engineering & technology as well as humanities & social sciences at graduate and post-graduate level. We endeavor to create a safe social and physical environment which helps all our students learn and succeed. This campus uniquely stands to promote academia-industry linkage focused on socio- economic development of Pakistan and creation of sustainable R&D ecosystem that will enable the Public and Corporate sector industry to flourish.

## Welcome to International Cooperation Office
Air University
The International Cooperation Office (ICO), established in 2008, plays a vital role in promoting the internationalization of higher education, research, and innovation at Air University. Through global partnerships, exchange programs, collaborative research, and international conferences, the ICO continues to strengthen AU‚Äôs global presence and academic linkages. The management at Air University also realizes that International educational cooperation is a mean for enhancing and fostering an international atmosphere on the university‚Äôs campuses, thus promoting personal growth and understanding of global responsibility among university members. 
  

* * *
##### Message from Director | ICO

**Mr. Umair Ahmad**  
Addl. Director | International Cooperation Office 
At Air University, we are dedicated to cultivating a dynamic and globally connected academic environment. The International Cooperation Office (ICO) actively fosters partnerships with leading institutions worldwide, providing students, faculty, and industry partners with opportunities to engage in transformative educational, research, and development initiatives.

# ONLINE SYSTEMS
#### [Admission Portal](https://kcportals.au.edu.pk/ADMISSIONS/)
Faculty members are encouraged to shape the educational programmes and curriculum offered by the institution using their knowledge and research.
#### [Job Portal](https://portals.au.edu.pk/JOBS/)
The majority of Job portals ask different things of employers in order for them to post job openings and respond to resumes.
#### [Fee Portal](https://kcportals.au.edu.pk/feesystem/)
Fee Portal offers information on fees for enrolled students, and a communications platform will provide a Challan form for payments made to banks.
#### [Student Portal](https://kcportals.au.edu.pk/students/)
The student Portal also offers details about the courses that are offered, transcripts, email services, timetables, and exam schedules.
#### [Leave Portal](https://kcportals.au.edu.pk/leavems/)
The approval of leave requests is expedited by the use of an online leave system. There are features like a leaving record and email notifications.
# AFFILIATED INSTITUTES
###  [**Bilquis College Nur Khan Base, Rawalpindi**](https://kc.au.edu.pk/Pages/AffilatedInstitutes/introduction.aspx)
The institution has been a focal point for the operations of the Pakistan Air Force Women Association (PAFWA) as well as for the education and training of women since it was founded in 1984.
###  [**College of Education, Peshawar**](https://kc.au.edu.pk/Pages/AffilatedInstitutes/introduction.aspx)
The Institute is in a unique position to equip teachers for secondary schools as well as Montessori institutes.
###  [**Aero Medical Institute, PAF Base, Masroor, Karachi**](https://kc.au.edu.pk/Pages/AffilatedInstitutes/introduction.aspx)
The largest airfield used by the Pakistan Air Force is PAF Base Masroor. The Sindh province's Mauripur neighbourhood of Karachi is where it is located.
###  [**Fazaia College of Education for Women, Lahore**](https://kc.au.edu.pk/Pages/AffilatedInstitutes/introduction.aspx)
FCoE(W), Lahore's rigorous educational and social environment not only produces great academic results, but also well-groomed citizens who can adapt to the diversity of the global community.
###  [**College of Education for Women, Peshawar**](https://kc.au.edu.pk/Pages/AffilatedInstitutes/introduction.aspx)
The college has provided public schools and Educational institutions with highly educated, informed, and skilled teachers.
# AU CAMPUSES
ESTABLISHED DATE : 
###  [ **ISLAMABAD CAMPUS** ](http://au.edu.pk/)
The campus is located near the Margalla foothills in the south east corner of sector E-9 (PAF Complex) of Islamabad. The University is a degree awarding autonomous institution and its graduates are offered good placement opportunities in the job market. 
[ VISIT WEBSITE ](http://au.edu.pk/) [ See More ](javascript:void\(0\);)
ESTABLISHED DATE : 
###  [ **KHARIAN CAMPUS** ](https://kc.au.edu.pk/)
Established in 2024, Air University Kharian Campus stands as a symbol of academic growth and innovation. The modern, purpose-built campus provides a vibrant learning environment where dedicated faculty guide students to achieve academic excellence and professional success. It currently offers undergraduate programs in Management Sciences (BBA and BS Accounting & Finance) and Computing (BS Computer Science, BS Cyber Security, and BS Artificial Intelligence), along with MS programs in Management and Computer Science. The campus remains committed to advancing research, innovation, and quality education in the region. 
[ VISIT WEBSITE ](https://kc.au.edu.pk/) [ See More ](javascript:void\(0\);)
ESTABLISHED DATE : 
###  [ **Aerospace & Aviation Campus Kamra** ](https://aack.au.edu.pk/)
The Campus is a great model of Academia-Industry-R&D linkage in Pakistan due to proximity of AU Kamra, PAC and NASTP Kamra. AU Kamra, as vital organ of National Aerospace City Kamra, has all the potential to contribute significantly towards muchdesired academia industry collaboration. The Campus has about 1200 enrolled students and currently running a total of 21 degree programs at undergraduate, graduate and postgraduate levels in engineering/non-engineering disciplines. The Campus boasts of Aerospace Engineering and Avionics Engineering as its niche disciplines. The campus has specialized faculty available in all Departments as per HEC requirements. 
[ VISIT WEBSITE ](https://aack.au.edu.pk/) [ See More ](javascript:void\(0\);)
ESTABLISHED DATE : 
###  [ **MULTAN CAMPUS** ](http://aumc.edu.pk/)
Air University Multan Campus is committed to delivering excellence in higher education and research. The campus offers a dynamic learning environment that integrates academic rigor with practical relevance, preparing students to meet the evolving demands of the global marketplace. With a team of highly qualified and experienced faculty, it emphasizes innovation, critical thinking, and professional competence. Equipped with state-of-the-art classrooms, advanced laboratories, and cutting-edge teaching technologies, the campus provides an inspiring academic setting that nurtures creativity and lifelong learning. It continues to play a pivotal role in the socioeconomic development of the region by fostering knowledge, leadership, and innovation. 
[ VISIT WEBSITE ](http://aumc.edu.pk/) [ See More ](javascript:void\(0\);)
ESTABLISHED DATE : 
###  [ **AU H-11 Campus Islamabad** ](https://au.edu.pk/)
Air University‚Äôs new state-of-the-art H-11 Campus is set to become operational from the Fall 2025 semester. Designed to meet modern academic and research needs, the campus will offer BS, MS, and PhD programs in Business Studies, Social Sciences, and Aerospace & Strategic Studies. With a capacity to accommodate over 7,000 students, the purpose-built facility reflects the university‚Äôs commitment to excellence in education and innovation. This milestone marks a significant expanding Air University‚Äôs academic footprint in the capital. 
[ VISIT WEBSITE ](https://au.edu.pk/) [ See More ](javascript:void\(0\);)
ESTABLISHED DATE : 
###  [ **Karachi CAMPUS** ](https://khi.au.edu.pk/)
Air University extends its legacy of excellence to Pakistan‚Äôs financial and commercial hub with the establishment of its Karachi Campus in 2025. Offering diverse programs aligned with national regulations and global standards, the campus provides state-of-the-art laboratories, modern classrooms, and digital learning facilities that foster innovation, research, and entrepreneurship. Ranked No. 2 in Pakistan and among the 600‚Äì800 universities globally by Times Higher Education (THE), Air University continues to empower Pakistani Minds for Global Leadership in the Innovation Economy. 
[ VISIT WEBSITE ](https://khi.au.edu.pk/) [ See More ](javascript:void\(0\);)
ESTABLISHED DATE : 
###  [ **AU Bahu Campus, Shorkot Cantt** ](https://sk.au.edu.pk/)
Air University expands its legacy of excellence to Central Punjab with the Future Projects of its Bahu Campus Shorkot Cantt in 2026. Strategically positioned to serve the Faisalabad, Jhang, and Sahiwal regions, the campus aims to bridge the educational gap in underserved areas through a mix of accredited and emerging programs aligned with technological growth and market demands. By launching flagship programs and fostering a niche for innovation and applied learning, the campus strengthens AU‚Äôs brand presence in the region. Ranked No. 2 in Pakistan and among the 600‚Äì800 universities globally by Times Higher Education (THE), Air University continues to empower Pakistani minds for global leadership in the innovation economy through its state-of-the-art infrastructure, modern laboratories, and highly qualified faculty. 
[ VISIT WEBSITE ](https://sk.au.edu.pk/) [ See More ](javascript:void\(0\);)

# URL: https://webdata.au.edu.pk/Pages/Academics/index.aspx





# Academics Department
Fostering innovation through an enriching academic ecosystem
## Our Motto
‚ÄúEmpowering minds through a dynamic educational ecosystem that ensures a pleasant and conducive learning and workplace environment for students and faculty by embracing a student-centric approach without compromising on the quality of education‚Äù. 
## Introduction
The Academics Department is Air University's academic hub. It coordinates and integrates various academic operations across the university, its Campuses, Constituent Units, and Affiliated Colleges, ultimately aiming to enhance the quality of education. Its core operations include curriculum development, instructional delivery, formulation of academic rules and regulations, and interpretation of academic policies in line with those of the university and regulatory bodies. The office is also responsible for the accreditation of programs by relevant councils and obtaining No Objection Certificates from HEC for starting new programs. 
In addition to its primary duties, this office provides academic support to other core operations of the university, such as exams, registration, admissions, automation, the quality enhancement cell, and graduate studies. The office facilitates the implementation of market-driven academic programs, focus on improving the skill set of graduates, contribute to the country's economic development, belong to emerging technological domains, and encourage innovation and creativity. Director Academics also oversees the AU Central Library.

# CONSTITUENT UNITS
###  [**Fazaia Medical College, Islamabad**](https://fazaiamedical.edu.pk/)
Fazaia Medical College was formally established on 16th March, 2015 and was inaugurated in December, 2015 with the start of first academic year. The college is located in the premises of Air University in a secure and scenic environment of PAF Complex E-9 and Margalla foothills. It is built on an atrium concept of architecture to ensure a conducive and congenial environment for education. The college has highly qualified and well experienced faculty. 
###  [**Fazaia Ruth Pfau Medical College, Karachi**](https://frpmc.edu.pk/)
The focus of health care‚Ä¶ has shifted from the individual to the community, from cure of disease to preservation of health, from episodic care to continuous and comprehensive care, and from an individual approach, provided by single primary care physicians, to comprehensive, community-based care, provided by primary-care teams‚Ä¶ These changes have significant implications for educational institutions.
###  [**College of Flying Training, Risalpur**](https://khi.au.edu.pk/Pages/College_of_flying_tranng/CFT_Intro.aspx)
With pride and enthusiasm, I welcome you to the esteemed College of Flying Training (CFT), a crucible for aviation's future leaders. As architects of transformation, we nurture pilots, controllers, defense officers, and logisticians through rigorous Aviation Management programs that transcend convention. Rooted in outcome-based education, we foster critical thinking and holistic growth, while instilling ethical and civic responsibility. Our vision is to excel in aviation management, driven by distinguished faculty and state-of-the-art facilities.
###  [**NASTP Institute of Information Technology (NIIT), Lahore**](https://niit.edu.pk/)
At NIIT University, we empower the next generation of tech visionaries through transformative education, advanced innovation, and research that drives the future. Our commitment goes beyond traditional learning; we foster a dynamic ecosystem where creativity meets cutting-edge technology, enabling students to tackle real-world challenges with confidence and expertise.

### [**AU Bahu Campus Shorkot Cantt.**](https://sk.au.edu.pk/)
Air University expands its legacy of excellence to Central Punjab with the Future Project of its Bahu Campus Shorkot Cantt in 2026. Strategically positioned to serve the Faisalabad, Jhang, and Sahiwal regions, the campus aims to bridge the educational gap in underserved areas through a mix of accredited and emerging programs aligned with technological growth and market demands. By launching flagship programs and fostering a niche for innovation and applied learning, the campus strengthens AU‚Äôs brand presence in the region. Ranked No. 2 in Pakistan and among the 600‚Äì800 universities globally by Times Higher Education (THE), Air University continues to empower Pakistani minds for global leadership in the innovation economy through its state-of-the-art infrastructure, modern laboratories, and highly qualified faculty.

## About the Journal
### Corporum: Journal of Corpus Linguistics
Corporum: Journal of Corpus Linguistics, the first journal of corpus linguistics in Pakistan is biannual and double blind peer reviewed journal published by Corpus Research Centre, Department of English, Air University, Islamabad, Pakistan.
#### Objectives
  * To provide national and international visibility to corpus-based researches
  * To give visibility to Pakistani (national and regional) languages at national and international level
  * To provide the opportunity to national and international scholars to publish their corpus-based researches
  * To promote research culture in Pakistan in the field of corpus linguistics
  * To establish institutional linkages with the universities of the world engaged in corpus-based research.


You may submit your research papers through Open Journal System (OJS). For all the queries regarding the call for papers and submission of research articles, you can email **cjcl@au.edu.pk****.**
##  Current Issue 
Vol. 8 No. 2 (2025): Corporum Journal of Corpus Linguistics 
Vol. 8 No. 2 (2025): Corporum Journal of Corpus Linguistics 
  * **P-ISSN 2617-2917**
  * **E-ISSN 2707-787X**
  * **Corpus Research Center (CRC)**
  * **Department of English**
  * **Air University, Islamabad**


Corporum: Journal of Corpus Linguistics, the first journal of corpus linguistics in Pakistan, is a biannual and double-blind peer-reviewed journal. It is published by the Corpus Research Centre, Department of English, Air University, Islamabad, Pakistan.
The advancement of technology in the field of linguistics has offered new avenues to researchers to use corpora in various disciplines. Corporum: Journal of Corpus Linguistics is a double-blind peer-reviewed journal that aims to create new research territory for corpus-based research at national and international levels. This journal aims to publish novel research on issues related to the real world of spoken and written data around the globe. Hence, the journal intends to address this large collection of linguistic data by engaging scholars from multidisciplinary fields, especially from computational/machine learning, the Sciences and the Humanities. Furthermore, it would provide a platform to voicing the researchers who are working and developing a corpus of various languages.
Published:  2025-12-31

## About the Journal
**Erevna: Journal of Linguistics and Literature is a blind peer-reviewed** journal that publishes original and high-quality research papers in various areas of linguistics and literature. Social scientists and investigators can distinguish the most up-to-date academic developments as a vital academic exchange platform and pursue indispensable crucial foundations for reference.
The paper should deal with the latest developments in linguistics and literature. As the journal has a uniquely broad coverage aiming to publish quality research in the relevant areas with an emphasis on interdisciplinary approaches in the analyses, we accept original papers addressing any aspect of linguistics and literature in the following areas:
**Phonetics, Phonology, Morphology, Semantics, Pragmatics, Syntax, Genre Studies, Corpus Linguistics, Sociolinguistics, Applied Linguistics, English Language Teaching, Discourse Analysis, Language Documentation, Trauma Studies, Perpetrators Studies, Feminism, Postcolonial Studies, Eco- Criticism, and Memory Studies.**
Our mission is to showcase quality research being carried out in literature and linguistics in Pakistan and around the world. This is hoped to be done by the contributions of researchers from a variety of theoretical and methodological perspectives.
##  Current Issue 
Vol. 9 No. 2 (2025): Erevna: Journal of Linguistics & Literature Volume 9 Issue 2

####  About Air University Multan Campus 
As a federally chartered, public sector university, AIR University can operate all over Pakistan. Southern Punjab consists of four divisions, Multan, Sahiwal, Bahawalpur and Dera Ghazi Khan. Large numbers of students from this region desiring higher education in Management Sciences and Computer Engineering move to educational institutions in Lahore, Islamabad or Karachi. 
The city of Multan is well placed to serve not only these four divisions, but also adjoining areas in Sind, Balochistan and Khyber-Pakhtunkhwa. In view of the heavy pressure of students seeking admission to courses of the kind offered by AIR University, the Prime Minister directed for the establishment of the Multan Campus of the University. The management conducted a feasibility study and decided to set up two faculties, Applied and Basic Sciences and Administrative Sciences in Phase I, to be followed by Engineering in Phase II. The University started the Multan Campus in the heart of the city in a rented building named Khan Centre at Abdali Road, Multan Cantt. In the fullness of time the campus will be constructed over an area of 200 acres in the suburbs of Multan. 
The University announced admission for two programs, BSCS and BBA (Honors) in the month of January 2011 and classes for these programs started on April 19, 2011. From Fall 2011 semester a third degree program, MBA (3 ¬Ω years), is also being offered. 
The campus is closely linked with the parent departments of the main campus and have worked a regular mechanism of knowledge sharing with them. The Multan campus is linked through PERN with the main campus. The facility of teleconferencing is provided. Therefore the class lectures of Islamabad campus and scholars of international repute are supplemented. 
The efforts are underway to hire highly qualified and professionally experienced teachers in the fields of finance, marketing, management and computer science. A computer lab has been established at the campus with internet facility. This computer lab is connected with HEC digital library. The students of these programs have almost unlimited access to the computer and professional software tools and other facilities of the main campus. The library of the campus is going to be established with the latest books in all areas of management sciences and computer science.

### Exemption Criteria
#### For All Engineering Programs:
As per PEC revised criteria for admission in Engineering programs, exemption is awarded on the basis of following pre-qualification of test: NAT-IE, NAT-ICS, USAT-E, USAT-CS (For HSSC in Computer Related Group), Entrance Tests conducted by UET Lahore, NED-UET Karachi, MUET Jamshero, NUST Islamabad , ETEA-KPK & HEC USAT-E. 
#### For All Computer Studies Related Programs
Exemption awarded on the basis of NAT-ICS, NAT-IE ,NAT-IM,USAT-E, USAT-M & USAT-CS 
#### For All Business/ Management Studies Related Programs
At least 1100 in SAT-1 OR All 6 types of NAT / USAT 
#### BS Physics
Exemption awarded on the basis of NAT-ICS, NAT-IM, NAT-IE, USAT-E, USAT-CS & USAT-M. 
#### BS Mathematics
Exemption awarded on the basis of NAT-ICS, NAT-IGS, NAT-IE, USAT-E, USAT-CS & USAT-GS. 
#### BS English, Psychology & International Relations
All 6 types of NAT / USAT 
**Note:**
  1. - Pre-qualified NAT/USAT must relate to candidate's HSSC qualification
  2. - Minimum 50 score is required for exemption
  3. - Test must be passed with in last one year from AU closing date of Admission.

  
Aggregate Merit Formulation Criteria for UG Programs   
---  
For Engineering Programs   
SSC/ Equivalent (%)  | HSSC/ Equivalent (%)  | Entrance Test (%)  | Total (%)   
10 %  | 50 %  | 40 %  | 100 %   
For Non-Engineering Programs   
15 %  | 35 %  | 50 %  | 100 %   
Aggregate Merit Formulation Criteria for MBA / MS / M.Phil Programs   
Terminal Degree Weightage (%)  | Entrance Test (%)  | Total (%)   
50 %  | 50 %  | 100 %   
  

#### MBA/MS Candidates:
NTS GAT-General/HEC-HAT Test with relevant category (at least 50 score). 
#### PhD Candidates:
NTS GAT-Subject Test (at least 60 score).

  * [Bachelor of Science International Relations (BS-IR)](https://webdata.au.edu.pk/Pages/Admission/eligibility_criteria.aspx#collapse1-19)
The Intermediate (Part I and II) examination of any Board of Intermediate and Secondary Education in Pakistan. Applicants must have scored 50% or more marks.
**OR**
An examination equivalent to Intermediate. Such candidates are required to submit an Equivalence Certificate issued by the Inter Board Chairman Committee, Islamabad, before the semester starts. This certificate must indicate the marks equivalent to marks in the Intermediate examination.
**OR**
The GCE 'A' level examination with three subjects. Such candidates are required to submit an Equivalence Certificate issued by the Inter Board Chairman Committee, Islamabad, before the semester starts. This certificate must indicate the marks equivalent to marks in the Intermediate examination.
Applicants awaiting results may be given provisional admission until the declaration of their respective results. Only those scoring 50% or more marks shall be considered. Those scoring less than 50% marks shall have their provisional admissions cancelled and shall be withdrawn from their respective programs.
Applicants scoring minimum passing marks in the Intermediate or in GCE ‚ÄòA‚Äô level or in any other examination equivalent to the intermediate are eligible for admission. Those getting partial pass results due to any reason, or who are required to appear in compartment/supplementary paper(s), are not eligible for admission even if their aggregate marks are 50% or more in their respective examination.
The absolute value of percentage is considered as final; it is not rounded off to the next whole number, e.g., 49.9% is considered 49.9% and NOT 50%.

  * [Bachelor of Electrical Engineering / Bachelor of Mechatronics Engineering / Bachelor of Mechanical Engineering / Bachelor of Computer Engineering](https://webdata.au.edu.pk/Pages/Admission/eligibility_criteria.aspx#collapse1-2)
Applicants must have passed: Intermediate (Part I and II) examination with Physics, Chemistry & Mathematics from any Board of Intermediate and Secondary Education in Pakistan. In addition, a combination of Physics, Mathematics and Computer Studies/ Computer Science (ICS) is also allowed for admission in all Engineering Programs with Chemistry as remedial subject/ course in 1st Semester after admission. Applicant must have scored ‚â•60% marks.
**OR**
An examination equivalent to Intermediate. Such candidates are required to submit an Equivalence Certificate issued by the Inter Board Chairman Committee (IBCC), Islamabad before the semester starts. This certificate must indicate obtained equivalent marks in Intermediate.
**OR**
GCE ‚ÄòA‚Äô level examination with three subjects (Physics, Chemistry & Mathematics) or combination of Physics, Mathematics & Computer Studies/ Computer Science (ICS) is also allowed for admission in all Engineering Programs with Chemistry as remedial subject/ course in 1st Semester after admission The candidates are required to submit an Equivalence Certificate issued by the Inter Board Chairman Committee (IBCC), Islamabad before the semester starts. This certificate must indicate obtained equivalent marks in Intermediate.
Applicants awaiting results shall be given provisional admission until declaration of their respective results. Applicants scoring 60%. or more marks shall only begranted admission. Those scoring less than 60% marks shall have their provisional admission cancelled and they shall be withdrawn from their respective program. Upon announcement of results, only those applicants shall be granted admission, who pass ALL the subjects and score at least 60% marks. Applicants getting partial pass result, due to any reason, or required to appear in compartment / supplementary paper(s) shall not be eligible for admission, even if their aggregate marks are 60% or more.
Applicants awaiting results shall be given **PROVISIONAL ADMISSION** until declaration of results from respective Boards/ Examination body. Applicants scoring ‚â•60% shall only be granted admission. Those scoring less than 60% marks shall have their provisional admission cancelled and they shall be withdrawn from their respective program immediately. Upon announcement of results, only those applicants shall be granted admission, who pass all subjects and score at least 60% marks. Applicants getting partial pass result, due to any reason, or required to appear in compartment / supplementary paper(s) shall not be eligible for admission, even if their aggregate marks are 60% or more.
The absolute value of percentage is considered as final; it is not rounded off to the next whole number, e.g., 59.9% is considered 59.9% and NOT 60%.

**Eligibility Criteria**
The applicant is required to meet the following minimum eligibility requirements:
**Degree Requirement:**
Prior to admission into a PhD program, the student shall have been awarded MS/MPhil or equivalent degree as described in this policy. Where necessary, the candidate may be admitted in Zero Semester to clear the deficient course of 9-12 Credit Hours, if/ as determined by the Departmental Admission Committee. Passing of Deficient courses with min 3.0/4.0 is mandatory in maximum two chances. The Zero Semester would not be counted towards maximum degree duration.
**Entry Test:**
Pass the Air University (equivalent to Graduate Record Examination GRE/Higher Education Aptitude Test (HAT in relevant category) with a passing score of 60% OR Pass an equivalent test conducted by Air University OR conducted by testing bodies accredited / recognized by HEC.
**Cumulative Grade Point Average (CGPA):**
(a) For admission in a PhD program, a minimum CGPA of 3.00 (out of 4.00) or 60% (in the annual system degree awarded in percentage %) in the MS/MPhil/equivalent degree being considered for admission, is required, whether such degree was obtained from Pakistani or foreign universities.
(b) If the CGPA/Percentage is not mentioned on the transcript, the candidate must produce equivalent weightage from the degree awarding university. 
(c) A student having strong demonstrated interest in obtaining PhD degree, but with CGPA below 3.00 (out of 4.00 in the semester system) or 60% marks (in the annual system degree awarded in percentage %) in the most recent degree obtained, may be admitted to a PhD program after fulfilling the following requirements:- (i) Register and pass additional courses of 9-12 CH of level 7 (Masters level) taking a zero semester at the awarding university/HEI/DAI and core minimum 3.00 out of 4.00 GPA, (ii) Satisfy the admission committee that the applicant's knowledge of primary area (level 7; Masters) has sufficiently prepared him/her to undertake the course of studies of the doctoral program, and (iii) fulfil all other requirements set in this policy for admission to a PhD program.
**Statement of Purpose:**
All applicants are required to submit a Statement of Purpose along with the application form, writing clearly their intended research interest and preference/choice of Supervisor where applicable. The statement of purpose will include: (i) Title of the potential research proposal, (ii) Clear articulation of the current understanding of the intended field and ideas for potential research, and (iii) Explanation of the intended impact of the proposed research.
**Admission Requirement for Intradisciplinary Degree Holders:**
The candidate who is intended to admission in a PhD program at AU with intra-disciplinary qualification is required to pass GRE-Subject/Equivalent Test with minimum 50% marks in the discipline of admission and also required to pass 6-9 CH of deficiency courses of level 7 of relevant degree program. The candidate should have strong interest in pursuing a PhD in a different discipline. These requirements shall be in addition to any other requirements set in this policy for admission to a PhD program. In such a case, the candidate would not be a student of PhD program. Such candidates would be offered provisional admissions to MS/MPhil programs offered in Fall & Spring intakes to enable the candidates to apply for PhD programs where intradisciplinary candidates are accepted. Contingent upon this qualification with min 3.0/4.0 in max two chances to fulfil the deficiency requirement, the candidate would be required to apply for PhD program (as and when offered), Pass the GAT (Subject)/ or Equivalent Test with 60% marks and appear before admission committee prior to admission. Based on Departmental Admission Committee‚Äôs recommendation the candidate may be admitted in a PhD Program. The Committee may further determine (where required) the deficient/ essential course (s) to study in addition to required mandatory 18 Credit Hours to complete the course work.
**For specific eligibility requirement of any PhD degree program, please click on program title.**

#### _AU Sponsored MS & PhD Programs_
  

AU pays back to society through Graduate Research Initiative Program. This program enables the students to take on professional challenges for excellent leadership careers in academia and industry. This scheme offers following benefits for selected candidates.
  

#### _Scheme-I_
  

  * -A stipend of Rs. 40,000/- per month(In Engineering Depts. and Rs. 20,000 per Month in Faculty of Computing & Artificial Intelligence) 
  * -100% Tuition fee waiver
  * -Career progression through Lab Engineer, Teaching/ Research Assistant, Post-doc and faculty positions at Air University.
  * -Eligibility Criteria : ‚â• 3.5 CGPA in Bachelor Degree 
  * -A bond with University would be required. 

  

#### _Scheme-II_
  

  * -100% Tuition Fee Waiver 
  * -The selected students would be required to perform Teaching Assistant/ Research Assistant role with Dept. 
  * -Eligibility Criteria : ‚â• 3.5 CGPA in Bachelor Degree 
  * -A bond with concerned Dept.. would be required. 

  

#### _Scheme-III_
  

  * -50% Tuition Fee Waiver 
  * -The selected students would be required to perform in Dept. as assigned by the Head of Dept.
  * -Eligibility Criteria : ‚â• 3.0 CGPA in Bachelor Degree 


#### _Note:_
All fee waivers are subject to continued academic performance in semester studies. 
  

#### _Educate to Innovate Scholarship Scheme (Only for MS Information Security and MS Avionics Engg)_
  

  * -This scheme offers Full and Partial fee waiver to students with bright academic record. 
  * -Eligibility criteria is CGPA 3.00 or above in the relevant bachelor degree


Additionally the selected students would have following opportunities: 
  * -Chance to work as apprentice in industry projects after 1st semester for students with bright academic record and relevant skills
  * -The student will be working on Industry/Research Projects
  * -Data sharing for aerial vehicles
  * -GSM Security
  * -Sensor Fusion for mobile nodes

  

#### _NEED & MERIT BASED FINANCIAL AID SCHEMES_
  

In every Fall semester, AU invites applications from fresh entrants for financial grants at the time of applying for admission at AU portal. Based on the information provided by students, Financial Aid Office (FAO) prepares a list of needy/deserving students for financial grants. The scale of all need-based grants will depend on the availability of funds and would be reviewed periodically.
  

Following are categories of grants available to students at Air University:
  

  * (a) Ehsaas Undergraduate Scholarship Projects, EUSP) (If Govt/HEC offers scheme)
  * (b) HEC Need Based Grant (Subject to funding in recurring grant)
  * (c) Punjab Educational Endowment Fund (PEEF)
  * (d) Air University Need Based Financial Grant (AUNBFG)
  * (e) Incentive Financial Grant (IFG) to AU Multan Campus
  * (f) PAF Wards Discounts/Rebate
  * (g) AU Employee Discount 
  * (h) AU Employee Ward Discount/Rebate
  * (i) HEC Employee Ward Discount

  

#### _Procedure to Apply for Financial Grants_
  

  * 1. Following procedure would be followed: -
    * (a) All candidates who are applying for admission at AU in undergraduate program can also apply for financial grants on the prescribed form available with online- admission form while entering their personal and academic data. 
    * (b) After confirmation of admission, the students would be required to submit the necessary documents at Financial Aid Office within fifteen days of commencement of semester. 
    * (c) The students who missed to apply online at the time of Fall admissions can alsoapply to Registrar for financial grant on prescribed form within fifteen days of commencement of semester
    * (d) The students admitted in Spring semester would be eligible to apply for financial grant in the next fall semester on prescribed form.
  

#### _Eligibility Criteria_
  

  * 2. Following is eligibility criteria for award of financial grant to students: -
    * (a) Students admitted on open merit only are eligible for award of NBFG.
    * (b) Continuation of NBFG is subject to good conduct of the student and educational performance (minimum CGPA of 2.0) in the proceeding semesters. Financial Grant of the student having less than 2.0 CGPA will be discontinued and would be resumed only when student acquires CGPA ‚â• 2.0.
    * (c) Only one NBFG to student is permissible i.e., students availing any other need based financial grant or departmental grant or employee concession will not be eligible for award of second NBFG.
    * (d) In a repeat case of penalty due to use of unfair means case or act of indiscipline, a student would be ineligible for any NBFG/Scholarship in following semesters.
    * (e) Ehsaas Scholarship will be offered to students as per HEC defined criteria.
    * (f) Punjab Educational Endowment Fund (PEEF) will be offered as per PEEF defined criteria.
    * (g) HEC Need based financial grant will be awarded as per HEC criteria.
    * (h) PAF Ward discount/ rebate would be awarded 25% tuition fee rebate only on provision of requisite in-service/ retirement documents for normal degree duration only.
    * (i) AU Employee concession would be awarded 50% tuition fee rebate only with subject to meeting following conditions:- 
      * i. Employee is not on probation period. 
      * ii. In case of self-enrolment in a degree program, the employee would be required to produce NOC duly issued by HR department.
      * iii. The student is admitted on open merit in degree program
      * iv. Award is for normal degree duration only.
AU Incentive Financial Grant (IFG) for Multan Campus
  * 3. As per directives of the BOGs, students of AU Multan Campus are awarded incentive Financial Grant (IFG) on tuition fee which would be reviewed every year, keeping in view the availability of funds. HEC Employee Wad Discount
  * 4. Wards of HEC regular employee(but not on consultancy, contract or adhoc basis)would be awarded 50% Tuition Fee Concession for the complete degree program in the light of decision made in VCs Meeting held at HEC dated 7th August, 2004 (Ref: Item No 06). All such student would require to produce letter of employment of his/her father/mother from HEC HR Dept at the time of admission and letter on semester to semester basis.


#### _MERIT SCHOLARSHIPS POLICY_
  

Air University offers Merit based Scholarships to all outstanding students enrolled in different undergraduate and graduate programs based on their semester results.
  

#### _Undergraduate Students_
  

  * 1. In undergraduate programs following scholarships are awarded to top three position holders of each program of a batch as tuition fee waiver: -
    * (a) 1st Position Holder Rs. 25,000
    * (b) 2nd Position Holder Rs. 20,000
    * (c) 3rd Position Holder Rs. 15,000
    * (d) Students attaining SGPA of 4.0 will get Rs. 5,000 over and above. However, they would be included in the first three position holders in the class. Also, the total value of grant would not exceed from 100 percent of paid tuition fee through AU or any other documented sources. 
  

#### _Eligibility Criteria (for undergraduate students)_
  

  * 2. Following is qualifying criteria for the merit scholarship of UG students: -
    * (a) Students of all Undergraduate programs are eligible for grant of Merit scholarship.
    * (b) Students must score minimum SGPA of 3.5 to qualify for the award of Merit Scholarship.
    * (c) Full time students with full academic load in a regular semester will qualify for award of Merit Scholarship.
    * (d) Merit Scholarships will not be awarded for summer semester.
    * (e) Students having disciplinary punishment during the semester will be disqualified for the award of merit scholarship for next one semester including concerned semester.
    * (f) A student would be granted merit scholarship along with Need Based scholarship or any other fee rebate through AU or external sources due to their parents but the accumulative award amount shall not exceed from 100 percent of paid tuition fee.
    * (g) Final Semester i.e., graduating batch will not be awarded Merit Scholarship. 
    * (h) If there is a tie on first, second and third position between two or more students, calculated till two decimal points, all of them would receive financial reward of their respective positions however: they will be counted in position holders of the batch.
    * (i) In case of any conflict, Vice Chancellor‚Äôs decision would be final.
  

#### _Postgraduate Students (MBA/MS/M.Phil.)_
  

  * 3. In MBA/MS/ M.Phil. programs, scholarships are awarded to top three position holders of program of a batch for first two semesters only (with regular workload) in the shape of tuition fee waiver as shown below: -
    * (a) 1st Position Holder Rs. 25,000
    * (b) 2nd Position Holder Rs. 20,000
    * (c) 3rd Position Holder Rs. 15,000
  

#### _Eligibility Criteria (for MBA/MS/M.Phil. students)_
  

  * 4. Following is qualifying criteria for the merit scholarship for MBA/MS/M.Phil. students: -
    * (a) Students of all MBA/MS/M.Phil. Programs are eligible for Merit Scholarship.
    * (b) Students must score minimum of SGPA as 3.75 to qualify for the award of Merit Scholarship.
    * (c) Full time students with full academic load in a regular semester will qualify for the award of Merit Scholarship.
    * (d) Merit Scholarship will not be awarded for summer semester and thesis work duration.
    * (e) Students having disciplinary punishment during the semester will be disqualified for the award of merit scholarship for the next one semester including ongoing semester.
    * (g) If there is a tie on first, second and third position between two or more students, calculated till two decimals point, all of them would receive financial reward of their respective positions; however, they will be counted in position holders of the batch.
    * (h) The students enrolled in MS programs at AU on Gratis basis, as Research Assistant or on sponsorship (through AU or external sources), they would be counted towards merit position in the batch, but they shall be awarded only difference of merit scholarship amount and not exceeding 100% paid tuition fee.
    * (i) In case of any conflict, VC‚Äôs decision would be final.
  

#### _Procedure for Award of Merit Scholarship_
  

  * 5. Financial Aid Office would be responsible to process the case for award of merit scholarship to the eligible students within two months of declaration of semester final results. After finalization of merit scholarship, the students would be intimated by Financial Aid Office about the adjustment of award amount in fee or refund in the shape of payment draft. 


Any scholarship related information, please contact:- 
**Mr. Babar Hussain**  
**Financial Aid Officer**  
**Ext: 214 or 0519153214**  
**Email:fao@au.edu.pk**

# AU CAMPUSES
ESTABLISHED DATE : 
### [**ISLAMABAD MAIN CAMPUS**](http://au.edu.pk/)
[ VIST WEBSITE ](http://au.edu.pk/)
ESTABLISHED DATE : 
###  [**MULTAN CAMPUS**](http://aumc.edu.pk/)
In 2011, Air University established its second campus in Multan, Punjab, Pakistan. It offers undergraduate and postgraduate degree programs in management sciences, accounting and finance, information technology, mathematics and computer science. 
[VISIT WEBSITE ](http://aumc.edu.pk/)
ESTABLISHED DATE : 
The campus is established in close vacinity of Pakistan Aeronautical Complex Attock and will have linkeges with Aviation Research Inovation and Development (AVRID). Aviation Design Institution (AVDI) and National Aerospace Science and Technology Park (NASTP) . 
[VISIT WEBSITE ](https://aack.au.edu.pk/)
ESTABLISHED DATE : 
###  [**Karachi Campus**](https://khi.au.edu.pk/)
Air University has its footprints in Karachi through Fazaia Ruth Pfau Medical College (FRPMC), a consituent insittution of Air University, Islamabad. The College was established in 2019 at PAF Base Faisal. Named after the renowned humanitarian Dr. Ruth Pfau, the college offers a modern medical education aligned with national standards. With advanced facilities and strong clinical affiliations, FRPMC is committed to producing skilled and compassionate healthcare professionals. 
[VISIT WEBSITE ](https://khi.au.edu.pk/)
ESTABLISHED DATE : 
### [**KHARIAN CAMPUS**](https://portals.au.edu.pk/kharian_Campus)
Air University Kharian Campus was established as part of the university's expansion efforts and officially opened around early 2024. It features modern facilities and a focus on research collaboration through proximity to the National Aerospace Science and Technology Park, aiming to boost educational opportunities and economic development in the Kharian area. 
  
[ VISIT WEBSITE ](https://kc.au.edu.pk/)
ESTABLISHED DATE : 
### [**Air University H-11 Campus**](https://au.edu.pk/)
  
[ VISIT WEBSITE ](https://au.edu.pk/)
FUTURE PROJECT : 
###  [**Bahu Campus, Shorkot Cantt**](https://sk.au.edu.pk/)
[VISIT WEBSITE ](https://sk.au.edu.pk/)

#### Vision:
The Counseling Center strives to provide helpful and effective counseling services that are accessible to all regular university students. We believe in creating a welcoming environment that values diversity and encourages intellectual and emotional growth along with a focus at fostering personal & social learning and development.
#### Mission:
The Counseling Center‚Äôs mission is to provide high quality counseling services to students who are struggling with personal, academic, or social concerns. We aim to support the learning environment of the University by promoting positive mental health for students through individual and group counseling, crisis intervention, consulting and referral, assessment, and outreach programming that are responsive to the individual, cultural, and demographic diversity of our students.

#### CPEC Center of Excellence at Air University School of Management, Islamabad was established in Feb 2018.
Establishment Ceremony of ‚ÄúCPEC Center of Excellence at Air University School of Management‚Äù was held in Islamabad (main) campus of Air University.
**Minister of State and Chair Board of Investment Mr. Naeem Y. Zamindar inaugurated the center.**
Prof. Dr. Idrees Khawaja (Dean Air University School of Management), Mr. Muhammad Saleem Ranjha (Additional Secretary/ Executive Director General BOI), AVM (R) Tariq Matin (Director Academics), Air Cdre (R) Muhammad Saleem (Registrar AU), Air Cdre (R) Afzaal Ahmad (Director ORIC), Air Cdre (R) Abdul Wahab Motla (Director QEC), Dr. S. K. Shahzad (Head CPEC Center AU) were present at the occasion.
On behalf of Air University Prof. Dr. Idrees Khawaja delivered the welcome speech. He suggested that establishment of CPEC Center of Excellence at AU was an important step and would have significant and positive impact on CPEC related research. Other senior officials representing AU had also ensured that center shall play its role in promoting research relating international business especially Export Processing Zones.
Mr. Naeem Y. Zamindar, said that he assigned high value to CPEC Centers of Excellence in Pakistan, especially the ones that operate at the universities‚Äô level. He hoped that scholarly community of China and Pakistan, through these Centers shall increase the overall cooperation to give boost to the science and technology.
#### Projects at CPEC Center of Excellence AUSOM
‚úì For Pakistan, China-Pak Economic Corridor (CPEC) is a fate changer. Technically this south Asian developing country will act as an Entrepot to China. In this newly developing contextual setting, Export Processing Zones (EPZs) will have significant implications not only for the economy of Pakistan but also for the economy of whole globe. Apart from economic contributions, EPZs‚Äîas an important tool to promote international trade‚Äîare expected to contribute towards human welfare in Pakistan. 
Therefore, CPEC Center of Excellence at AU, aims to understand how the contribution of EPZs towards human welfare, in post-CPEC scenario can be maximized in Pakistan. Towards this end, a project tilted ‚ÄúPositioning for Maximal Gain: How the Human Welfare Output of Export Processing Zones in a Developing Country‚Äôs context can be maximized?‚Äù was proposed to Higher Education Commission (HEC) of Pakistan. HEC has approved Rs. 1.76 Million for completion of this project in 30 months.
Successful completion of this project shall help Ministry of Industries, Planning Commission of Pakistan, Ministry of Climate Change, Export Processing Zones Authority etc. Moreover, export related industries‚Äîtextile steel, hi-tech industry, gem & jewelry, software houses, information technology based industries, precession engineering, blister, copper, gold, lead and zinc, steel billets, direct reduced Iron (DRI) and many other industries listed on official website of Export Processing Zones Authority (EPZA) will indirectly benefit from this study Please See: <http://www.epza.gov.pk>
‚úì In another project, CPEC Center of Excellence at AUSOM is also helping Ministry of Overseas Pakistanis (Overseas Pakistani Foundation) in establishing the state of the art university in Islamabad Pakistan.

#### Transfer of Program within AU
Transfer to another program is generally discouraged but under special circumstances an enrolled student may apply for transfer from one program to another, in the first two semesters of the program. The application is to be submitted to the respective Chair Department at least two weeks before the start of the semester in which the student is seeking a program transfer. Only students with CGPA of at least 3.0 may apply.

####  Our Vision:
AUSOM aspires to nurture visionary leadership within a dynamic educational ecosystem where ingenuity thrives, global perspectives converge, and ethical conduct drives industry and society. 
####  Our Mission:
AUSOM is committed to progressive education and research, fostering interdisciplinary engagement, critical thinking, entrepreneurship, and a culture of social responsibility to cultivate a new generation of leaders capable of addressing national and global challenges.
####  Our Values:
Integrity, Rigor, Experiential learning, Collaboration, Diversity

# QEC POLICY
* * *
### QA POLICY STATEMENT
Air University Quality Assurance Policy Statement Air University will serve the community and meet the challenging needs of national and international market by providing quality higher education through effective and efficient quality assurance system underpinned by quality teaching, learning and research. University will also inculcate ethical values in students through its programs to become better citizens. 
### SALIENT FEATURES
The university in this QA System has adopted quality as "Fitness for Purpose" a concept that stresses the need to meet or conform to generally accepted standards defined by Higher Education Commission. 
### OBJECTIVES
Effective Institutional quality assurance processes assess quality against their mission and related objectives. The university in this QA System has adopted quality as "Fitness for Purpose" a concept that stresses the need to meet or conform to generally accepted standards defined by Higher Education Commission.

#### Federal Minister for Planning and Development inaugurated the Centre.
Federal Minister for Interior Ahsan Iqbal inaugurated the National Centre for Cyber Security (NCCS) on Monday, 21st May 2018 at Air University (AU) Islamabad. The minister said establishment of National Centre for Cyber Security was his dream which had now been fulfilled. 
Mr. Ahsan Iqbal (Federal Minister Planning Commission), Dr. Arshad Ali (Executive Director Higher Education Commission), Dr. Athar Osama (Member S&T & ICT Planning Commission), AVM (R) Faaiz Amir (Vice Chancellor Air University), AVM (R) Tariq Matin (Director Academics AU), Air Cdre (R) Muhammad Saleem (Registrar AU), Air Cdre (R) Afzaal Ahmad (Director ORIC AU), Prof. Dr. Kashif Kifayat (Director NCCS AU), other senior AU Officials, all directors of NCCS partner Labs, and numerous dignitaries were present at the occasion. 
Vice Chancellor Air University AVM (R) Faaiz Amir delivered the welcome speech. He articulated that NCCS would work as centre of excellence and create a significant impact for Cyber Security Research and Development in Pakistan. Other senior officials representing AU had mentioned that NCCS shall play positive role in promoting R&D Culture in specialized areas of Cyber Security. 
  
For more information please visit:[ http://www.nccs.pk ](http://www.nccs.pk/)

###  Welcome to our project "ReCyP:HER"!
The goal of the project "Rethinking Cybersecurity in Pakistan ‚Äì Human factors‚Äò Essential Role‚Äú, short RECYPHER, is to create a comprehensive capacity building in Pakistan for the area of cybersecurity and the connection with psychological know-how.
This project is funded by the European Union within the Erasmus+ program. The applicant, the Chair of Industrial and Organizational Psychology at Saarland University, is working together with the five project partners Lahore University of Management Sciences, National University for Sciences and Technology in Islamabad, Air University in Islamabad, the Institute of Business Administration in Karachi and the Cybersecurity Center at Boƒüazi√ßi University in Istanbul.
Cybercrime poses a major threat to the economic growth of developing countries. With the aim of using psychological know-how in the field of IT security, the project aims to raise awareness of cyber security issues and to promote the establishment of close networks between universities and IT security companies in Pakistan.
  

* * *
### Project Partners
* * *
**Saarland University**
**LUMS**
**Institute of Business Administration**
**Air University Islamabad**
  

**National University Of Sciences & Technology**
**Cybersecurity Center an der Boƒüazi√ßi University**
